2445Encorafenib</a>

2446 plus <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=793872&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000793872&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2447binimetinib</a>

2448.</li>

2449</ul>

2450</div>

2451</li>

2452<li>

2453<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=615576&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000615576&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2454Oncolytic virus therapy</a>

2455: A type of targeted therapy that is used in the treatment of melanoma. Oncolytic virus therapy uses a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45941&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045941&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2456virus</a>

2457 that infects and breaks down cancer cells but not normal cells. Radiation therapy or chemotherapy may be given after oncolytic virus therapy to kill more cancer cells.

2458<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=776628&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000776628&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2459Talimogene laherparepvec</a>

2460 is a type of oncolytic virus therapy made with a form of the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46366&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046366&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2461herpesvirus</a>

2462 that has been changed in the laboratory. It is injected directly into tumors in the skin and lymph nodes.</li>

2463<li>

2464<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46739&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046739&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2465Angiogenesis inhibitors</a>

2466: A type of targeted therapy that is being studied in the treatment of melanoma. Angiogenesis inhibitors block the growth of new <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45020&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045020&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2467blood vessels</a>

2468. In cancer treatment, they may be given to prevent the growth of new blood vessels that tumors need to grow.

2469</li>

2470</ul>

2471</div>

2472<p id="_415" tabindex="-1">

2473For patients with melanoma who are at high risk of the cancer coming back after it has been treated, there is a growing number of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45587&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045587&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2474adjuvant therapy</a>

2475 options which may be given to lower the

2476 risk. Adjuvant therapy may

2477 include <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=772606&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000772606&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2478immune checkpoint inhibitors</a>

2479 and combinations of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44829&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044829&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2480signal transduction inhibitors</a>

2481. </p>

2482<p id="_306" tabindex="-1">

2483New targeted therapies and combinations of therapies are being studied in the treatment of melanoma.</p>

2484<p id="_287" tabindex="-1">

2485See <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/drugs/melanoma" title="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/drugs/melanoma">

2486Drugs Approved for Melanoma</a>

2487 for more information.</p>

2492New types of treatment are being tested in clinical trials.

2493 </h3>

2494<p id="_214" tabindex="-1">

2495This summary section describes treatments that are being studied in clinical trials. It may not mention every new treatment being studied. Information about clinical trials is available from the <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials" title="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials">

2496NCI website</a>

2497.</p>

2498<section id="_339">

2499<h4 id="_337" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2500Vaccine therapy</h4>

2501<p id="_338" tabindex="-1">

2502<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=386223&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000386223&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2503Vaccine therapy</a>

2504 is a cancer treatment that uses a substance or group of substances to stimulate the immune system to find the tumor and kill it. Vaccine therapy is being studied in the treatment of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45138&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045138&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2505stage III melanoma</a>

2506 that can be removed by surgery.</p>

2507</section>

2509<section id="_334">

2510<h3 id="_335" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2511Treatment for melanoma may cause side effects.</h3>

2512<p id="_334_md_73" tabindex="-1">

2513For information about <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46580&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046580&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2514side effects</a>

2515 caused by treatment for cancer, see our <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/side-effects" title="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/side-effects">

2516Side Effects</a>

2517 page.</p>

2518</section>

2519<section id="_217">

2520<h3 id="_218" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2521Patients may want to think about taking part in a clinical trial.</h3>

2522<p id="_217_md_23" tabindex="-1">

2523For some patients, taking part in a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45961&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045961&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2524clinical trial</a>

2525 may be the best treatment choice. Clinical trials are part of the cancer research process. Clinical trials are done to find out if new cancer treatments are safe and effective or better than the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44930&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044930&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2526standard treatment</a>

2527.</p>

2528<p id="_217_md_24" tabindex="-1">

2529Many of today's standard treatments for cancer are based on earlier clinical trials. Patients who take part in a clinical trial may receive the standard treatment or be among the first to receive a new treatment.</p>

2530<p id="_217_md_25" tabindex="-1">

2531Patients who take part in clinical trials also help improve the way cancer will be treated in the future. Even when clinical trials do not lead to effective new treatments, they often answer important questions and help move research forward.</p>

2532</section>

2533<section id="_219">

2534<h3 id="_220" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2535Patients can enter clinical trials before, during, or after starting their cancer treatment.</h3>

2536<p id="_219_md_29" tabindex="-1">

2537Some clinical trials only include patients who have not yet received treatment. Other trials test treatments for patients whose cancer has not gotten better. There are also clinical trials that test new ways to stop cancer from <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46556&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046556&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2538recurring</a>

2539 (coming back) or reduce the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46580&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046580&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2540side effects</a>

2541 of cancer treatment.</p>

2542<p id="_219_md_30" tabindex="-1">

2543Clinical trials are taking place in many parts of the country. Information about clinical trials supported by NCI can be found on NCI&#8217;s <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials/search" title="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials/search">

2544clinical trials search</a>

2545 webpage. Clinical trials supported by other organizations can be found on the <a href="https://clinicaltrials.gov/" title="https://clinicaltrials.gov/">

2546ClinicalTrials.gov</a>

2547 website.</p>

2548</section>

2549<section id="_221">

2550<h3 id="_222" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2551Follow-up tests may be needed.</h3>

2552<p id="_221_md_33" tabindex="-1">

2553Some of the tests that were done to <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46450&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046450&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2554diagnose</a>

2555 the cancer or to find out the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45885&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045885&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2556stage</a>

2557 of the cancer may be repeated. Some tests will be repeated in order to see how well the treatment is working. Decisions about whether to continue, change, or stop treatment may be based on the results of these tests.</p>

2558<p id="_221_md_34" tabindex="-1">

2559Some of the tests will continue to be done from time to time after treatment has ended. The results of these tests can show if your <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=651193&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000651193&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2560condition</a>

2561 has changed or if the cancer has <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46556&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046556&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2562recurred</a>

2563 (come back). These tests are sometimes called <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44671&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044671&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2564follow-up</a>

2565 tests or check-ups.</p>

2915 that target certain <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45693&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045693&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2916gene</a>

2917 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46063&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046063&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2918mutations</a>

2919. These may be given alone or in combination.</li>

2920<li>

2921Surgery to remove all known <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45333&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045333&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2922cancer</a>

2923.</li>

2924<li>

2925<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46559&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046559&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2926Regional chemotherapy</a>

2927 (<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45716&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045716&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2928hyperthermic</a>

2929 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44853&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044853&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2930isolated limb perfusion</a>

2931). Some patients may also have immunotherapy with <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45290&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045290&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2932tumor necrosis factor</a>

2933.</li>

2934<li>

2935<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=301626&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000301626&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2936Systemic chemotherapy</a>

2937.</li>

2938</ul>

2939</div>

2940<p id="_TrialSearch_400_19" tabindex="-1">

2941Use our <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials/search" title="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials/search">

2942clinical trial search</a>

2943 to find NCI-supported cancer clinical trials that are accepting patients. You can search for trials based on the type of cancer, the age of the patient, and where the trials are being done. <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials/" title="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials/">

2944General information</a>

2945 about clinical trials is also available.</p>

2946</div>

3041 <section id="_AboutThis_1">

3042

3043 <h2>

3044About This PDQ Summary</h2>

3045

3046 <div id="_section_AboutThis_1" class="pdq-sections">

3047<section id="_AboutThis_2">

3048<h3 id="_AboutThis_2_toc">

3049About PDQ</h3>

3050<p id="_AboutThis_3" tabindex="-1">

3051Physician Data Query (PDQ) is the National Cancer Institute's (NCI's) comprehensive cancer information database. The PDQ database contains summaries of the latest published information on cancer prevention, detection, genetics, treatment, supportive care, and complementary and alternative medicine. Most summaries come in two versions. The health professional versions have detailed information written in technical language. The patient versions are written in easy-to-understand, nontechnical language. Both versions have cancer information that is accurate and up to date and most versions are also available in <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/espanol/publicaciones/pdq" title="https://www.cancer.gov/espanol/publicaciones/pdq">

3052Spanish</a>

3053.</p>

3054<p id="_AboutThis_4" tabindex="-1">

3055PDQ is a service of the NCI. The NCI is part of the National Institutes of Health (NIH). NIH is the federal government&#8217;s center of biomedical research. The PDQ summaries are based on an independent review of the medical literature. They are not policy statements of the NCI or the NIH.</p>

3056</section>

3057<section id="_AboutThis_5">

3058<h3 id="_AboutThis_5_toc">

3059Purpose of This Summary</h3>

3060<p id="_AboutThis_6" tabindex="-1">

3061This PDQ cancer information summary has current information about the treatment of melanoma. It is meant to inform and help patients, families, and caregivers. It does not give formal guidelines or recommendations for making decisions about health care.</p>

3062</section>

3063<section id="_AboutThis_7">

3064<h3 id="_AboutThis_7_toc">

3065Reviewers and Updates</h3>

3066<p id="_AboutThis_8" tabindex="-1">

3067Editorial Boards write the PDQ cancer information summaries and keep them up to date. These Boards are made up of experts in cancer treatment and other specialties related to cancer. The summaries are reviewed regularly and changes are made when there is new information. The date on each summary ("Updated") is the date of the most recent change.

3068</p>

3069<p id="_AboutThis_9" tabindex="-1">

3070The information in this patient summary was taken from the health professional version, which is reviewed regularly and updated as needed, by the <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/publications/pdq/editorial-boards/adult-treatment" title="https://www.cancer.gov/publications/pdq/editorial-boards/adult-treatment">

3071PDQ Adult Treatment Editorial Board</a>

3072.

3073</p>

3074</section>

3075<section id="_AboutThis_10">

3076<h3 id="_AboutThis_10_toc">

3077Clinical Trial Information</h3>

3078<p id="_AboutThis_11" tabindex="-1">

3079A clinical trial is a study to answer a scientific question, such as whether one treatment is better than another. Trials are based on past studies and what has been learned in the laboratory. Each trial answers certain scientific questions in order to find new and better ways to help cancer patients. During treatment clinical trials, information is collected about the effects of a new treatment and how well it works. If a clinical trial shows that a new treatment is better than one currently being used, the new treatment may become "standard." Patients may want to think about taking part in a clinical trial. Some clinical trials are open only to patients who have not started treatment.

3080</p>

3081<p id="_AboutThis_12" tabindex="-1">

3082Clinical trials can be found online at <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials" title="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials">

3083NCI's website</a>

3084. For more information, call the <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/contact/contact-center" title="https://www.cancer.gov/contact/contact-center">

3085Cancer Information Service</a>

3086 (CIS), NCI's contact center, at 1-800-4-CANCER (1-800-422-6237).

3087</p>

3088</section>

3089<section id="_AboutThis_13">

3090<h3 id="_AboutThis_13_toc">

3091Permission to Use This Summary</h3>

3092<p id="_AboutThis_14" tabindex="-1">

3093PDQ is a registered trademark. The content of PDQ documents can be used freely as text. It cannot be identified as an NCI PDQ cancer information summary unless the whole summary is shown and it is updated regularly. However, a user would be allowed to write a sentence such as &#8220;NCI&#8217;s PDQ cancer information summary about breast cancer prevention states the risks in the following way: [include excerpt from the summary].&#8221;

3094</p>

3095<p id="_AboutThis_15" tabindex="-1">

3096The best way to cite this PDQ summary is:</p>

3097<p id="_AboutThis_21" tabindex="-1">

3098PDQ&#174; Adult Treatment Editorial Board. PDQ Melanoma Treatment. Bethesda, MD: National Cancer Institute. Updated &lt;MM/DD/YYYY&gt;. Available at: <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/types/skin/patient/melanoma-treatment-pdq" title="https://www.cancer.gov/types/skin/patient/melanoma-treatment-pdq">

3099https://www.cancer.gov/types/skin/patient/melanoma-treatment-pdq</a>

3100. Accessed &lt;MM/DD/YYYY&gt;. [PMID: 26389388]</p>

3101<p id="_AboutThis_16" tabindex="-1">

3102Images in this summary are used with permission of the author(s), artist, and/or publisher for use in the PDQ summaries only. If you want to use an image from a PDQ summary and you are not using the whole summary, you must get permission from the owner. It cannot be given by the National Cancer Institute. Information about using the images in this summary, along with many other images related to cancer can be found in <a href="https://visualsonline.cancer.gov/" title="https://visualsonline.cancer.gov/">

3103Visuals Online</a>

3104. Visuals Online is a collection of more than 3,000 scientific images.

3105</p>

3106</section>

3107<section id="_AboutThis_17">

3108<h3 id="_AboutThis_17_toc">

3109Disclaimer</h3>

3110<p id="_AboutThis_18" tabindex="-1">

3111The information in these summaries should not be used to make decisions about insurance reimbursement. More information on insurance coverage is available on Cancer.gov on the <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/managing-care" title="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/managing-care">

3112Managing Cancer Care</a>

3113 page.</p>

3114</section>

3119More information about contacting us or receiving help with the Cancer.gov website can be found on our <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/contact" title="https://www.cancer.gov/contact">

3120Contact Us for Help</a>

3121 page. Questions can also be submitted to Cancer.gov through the website&#8217;s <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/contact/email-us" title="https://www.cancer.gov/contact/email-us">
